Hoovie, i know in the big scheme of things you are young.But in todays scheme of things you are old.  Besides being a bit of an eclectic collector of things, i like to watch collectors and collections and collectables of different things. And we have now reached a stage where lots of collectables have reached their peak and are now starting to decline in price because the buyers are either getting too old or dying off or the new generations of collectors are not interested in them.  Look at lots of Hollywood collectables, they are decreasing in price because lots of people werent around when the TV shows and movies were made, and they dont know who the actors were. Look at the younger generations, they now collect Iphones and early computers and video games and consuls.  Look at Model T fords and some of the early cars, because people who now collect never grew up with the Model T and so many of the early cars they are not interested in them other than being a novelty. The same thing is happening today.   How many of the Millenials will be interested in early corvettes and trans ams and early mercs and beamers.Or will they be more interested in the Toyota Prius or Nissan Leaf or the Tesla S or the Tesla coupe or the other versions of electric cars that they have now been growing up with?  That is why i think you should keep the Tesla S, because when you are 50 or 60 years old, the Tesla  maybe a $500,000 car.
